 gaar par samiti kaa gathan pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne july main kiya tha, jab unke paas vitt mantralay kaa prabhaar tha
 The Finance Ministry on Saturday also expanded the scope of the subject for consideration of the expert committee on GAAR
 iskaa makasad isamen sabhi anivaasee kar daataaon ko samahit karnaa he
 The Finance Ministry statement said, "the draft report has recommended certain amendments to the Income Tax Act, 1961, issuing guidelines under the Income Tax Rules, 1962, issuing circulars clarifying the GAAR provision and some other steps
 " The statement said, "it has now been decided to expand the scope of the committee's terms of reference to include all non-resident tax payers in place of just foreign institutional investors (fiis)
" "tippaniyan The committee has sought opinion from the concerned party on the draft report by 15 September
 iske baad vah is maah ke aakhir tak antim report jamaa karegi
 The committee on GAAR was formed by Prime Minister Manmohan Singh in July, when he had charge of the Finance Ministry

 aspx bharat ne islamabad main bhartiya ucchayog ke aath adhikariyon ke khilaaf lagaae gaye jasusi or aatankwaadi gatividhiyon ko samarthan dene ke pakistan ke aaropon ko 'niraadhaar or pushtiheen' qaraar dete hue khaarij kar diya
 Due to these allegations, India has no other option but to recall these officers
 videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa vikaas swaroop ne tikhi pratikriya main kaha ki bhartiya adhikariyon ke khilaaf aarope baad main gadhakar lagaae gaye or unki koi galati nahin hone ke baavjood unhen nishaanaa banane kaa yah ek 'ashisht prayaas' he
 Earlier, a member of the Pakistan High Commission was caught red-handed last week for his involvement in anti-india activities
 bharat ne us tareeke par bhi kadaa virodh jataayaa he, jisamen aath bhartiya adhikariyon ke naam or photo ko chapa gaya or unki suraksha se samjhauta kiya gaya
 Four of these officers hold diplomatic passports
 pakistan ne daawa kiya ki bhartiya ucchayog ke adhikari baluchistan or sindh khaskar karachi main jasusi, vidhvansak or aatanki gatividhiyon ko sahyog dene, china pakistan aarthik paripath ko nuksaan pahunchane evam donon rajyon main asthirataa ko hawa dene jaise kaaryon main sanlipt the
 Asked whether the Indian authorities were being called back, Swaroop said that this is a procedural matter and the government will take necessary steps keeping all aspects of the situation in mind
 unhone suraksha ko ek praathamikta bataaya
 Swaroop said, "we completely reject the baseless and unconfirmed allegations made by Pakistan against some officials of the Indian High Commission in Islamabad
" sarkaar in aaropon se puri tarah inkaar karti he
 He said, "it is particularly regrettable that the Pakistani authorities preferred to make the allegations after recalling six of their officers from the Pakistan High Commission
" in adhikariyon main se kuch ke naam mahmud akhtar ne bhartiya adhikariyon ke samaksh liye the
 Akhtar is the officer of Pakistan High Commission who was caught red handed
 ' It is learned that India will call back eight diplomats as their security is compromised
 swaroop ne kaha ki 'galat rup se fansaae gaye' bhartiya adhikari donon deshon ke bich logon ke madhya tathaa vyapaar evam aarthik sampark badhaane kii disha main kaam kar rahe the
 He said, "allied activities of the High Commission are feared to be adversely affected by Pakistan's false allegations against them
" ' unhone kaha ki sarkaar us tareeke kaa kadai se virodh karti he jisamen aath bharatiyon ke naam evam photo chaape gaye jinamein se chaar ke paas rajanyik passport he
 This is against the fundamental rules of diplomatic practice and etiquette
 videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa ne kaha ki bhartiya adhikariyon ke khilaaf aarope unki suraksha ke prati hanikaarak hai
 Swaroop said, 'we hope that the Government of Pakistan will take all necessary steps to ensure the safety of not only these eight diplomats and officials but also other members of the High Commission and their families during their stay in Pakistan
 'tippaniyan Pakistan had withdrawn six of its officers amid involvement in a spy scandal by its High Commission staff
 pakistan ne pichley saptaah bhartiya ucchayog main adhikari surajeet singh ko avaanchit vyakti ghoshit kiya tha tathaa swaroop ne bataaya ki singh ko waapas bula liya gaya
 Swaroop said that Pakistan's baseless allegations have increased the risk to the peace and security of the region, which has arisen due to Pakistan's support to cross-border terrorism against neighbors
 unhone kaha ki pakistan samasya se puri tarah se inkaar karata he or anargal aarope lagaakar apni jimmedaariyon se batch jaataa he
 (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Foreign Ministry spokesperson Vikas Swaroop said in a sharp response that the charges against the Indian authorities were later fabricated and it was a 'rude attempt' to target them, despite no fault of theirs
 isse pehle pakistan ucchayog ke ek sadsy ko pichley hafte bharat virdohi gatividhiyon main shaamil hone par range haath pakadaa gaya tha
 India has also strongly protested the manner in which the names and photos of eight Indian officials were printed and their security compromised
 inamen se chaar adhikariyon ke paas rajanyik passport he
 Pakistan claimed that Indian High Commission officials were involved in activities such as espionage, subversive and terrorist activities in Balochistan and Sindh, especially Karachi, damaging the china-pakistan economic circuit and fueling instability in both states
 yah puche jane par ki kya bhartiya adhikariyon ko waapas bulaayaa ja rahaa he, swaroop ne kaha ki yah ek prakriyaagat maamla he tathaa sarkaar sthiti ke sabhi pahaluon ko dhyaan main rakhkar aavashyak kadam uthaaegi
 He called security a priority
 swaroop ne kaha, 'ham pakistan dwaara islamabad main bhartiya ucchayog ke kuch adhikariyon ke khilaaf lagaae gaye niraadhaar or bina pushtiwale aaropon ko puri tarah khaarij karte hai
 The government completely denies these allegations
 ' unhone kaha, 'yah visheshrup se khedjanak he ki pakistani adhikariyon ne apane chah adhikariyon ko paak ucchayog se waapas bulaane ke baad yah aarope lagaana pasand kiya
 Some of these officers were named by Mahmud Akhtar before the Indian authorities
 akhtar pakistan ucchayog kaa vah adhikari he, jise range haath pakadaa gaya tha
 ' pataa chalaa he ki bharat aath rajanyikon ko waapas bulaaegaa kyonki unki suraksha ke saath samjhauta kiya gaya he
 Swaroop said that the 'wrongly implicated' Indian officials were working towards increasing trade and economic contacts between the people and between the two countries
 unhone kaha, 'unke khilaaf pakistan ke galat aaropon ke kaaran ucchayog kii sambhddha gatividhiyon par pratikul prabhaav padane kii ashanka he
 He said the government strongly opposed the manner in which the names and photographs of eight Indians were printed, of which four have diplomatic passports
 yah rajanyik chalan evam shishtachar ke moolbhoot niyamon ke viruddh he
 a spokesman for the Ministry of External Affairs said that the allegations against Indian officials are harmful to their security
 swaroop ne kaha, 'ham ummid karte hai ki pakistan kii sarkaar na keval in aath rajanyikon evam adhikariyon balki ucchayog ke anya sadasyon evam unke pariwaron ke pakistan main rahane ke dauraan unki suraksha sunishchit karne ke liye sabhi aavashyak kadam uthaaegi
 Comments pakistan ne apane ucchayog ke karmchaariyon ke ek jasusi cond main sanliptata ke bich apane chah adhikariyon ko waapas bula liya tha

 swaroop ne kaha ki pakistan ke niraadhaar aaropon ke kaaran kshetra kii shanti or suraksha ke liye jokhim bad gaya he, jo padosiyon ke khilaaf seemaa paar aatankwaad ko pakistan dwaara diye jane vaale sahyog ke kaaran hi paidaa hua he
 He said that Pakistan completely denies the problem and shuns its responsibilities by making unwarranted allegations

 Ramzan 2019:ramajaan kaa maheenaa har musalmaan ke liye bahut mahatvapurn hota he, jisamen 30 dinon tak roje rakhe jate hai
 According to Islam, the whole of Ramadan is divided into three parts, the first, the second and the third is called Ashara
 ashara arabi kaa 10 number hota he
 In this way the first Ashra in the first 10 days (1–10) of Ramadan, the second Ashra in the second 10 days (11–20) and the third Ashra in the third day (21–30) are divided
 is tarah ramajaan ke maheene main 3 ashare hote hai
 The first Ashra is of Rahmat, the second Ashra is of Magafirat i
e
 forgiveness of sins and the third Ashra is to protect himself from the fire of Jahannam (hell)
 ramajaan ke maheene ko lekar paigambar mohammad ne kaha he, ramajaan kii shuruyaat main rahamat he, bich main magafirat yani maafee he or iske ant main jahannam (hell) kii aag se bachaav he
 In the first 10 days of Ramadan, Allah blesses those who offer Rosa prayers
 ramajaan ke bich yani duusare ashare main musalmaan apane gunahon se pavitra ho sakate hai
 At the same time, you can protect yourself from the fire of Jahannam in the last Ashtray, the last of Ramadan
 ramajaan ke 3 ashare or unka mahatv-1
 First Stage of Ramadan ('mercy') - The first 10 days of Ramadan month are of Rahmat
 rojaa namaaj karne waalon par allaah kii rahamat hoti he
 Muslims should help the poor by donating more and more to the Asher before Ramadan
 har ek insaan se pyaar or namrata kaa vyavhaar karnaa chahie
 2
 ramajaan kaa doosraa ashara (second Stage of Ramadan- 'forgiveness')-ramajaan ke 11wein roje se 20wein roje tak doosraa ashara chalata he
 This Ashra is of forgiveness
 is ashare main log ibaadat kar ke apane gunahon se maafee paa sakate hai
 According to Islamic belief, if a person apologizes to his sins (sins) in the second Ashara of Ramadan, then at this time Allah forgives his captors sooner than other days
 3
 Third Stage of Ramadan (third Stage of Ramadan 'nijat') - The third and last Ashra of Ramadan starts from the 21st day of the moon and runs till the 29th or 30th day of the moon
 ye ashara sabase mahatvapurn mana jaataa he
 The purpose of the third Ashara is to protect oneself from the fire of Jahannam (hell)
 is dauraan har musalmaan ko jahannam se bachane ke liye allaah se dua kerani chahie
 In the last ashram of Ramadan, many Muslim men and women sit in ehtakaf
 bataa den, ehtakaaf main muslim purush masjid ke kone main 10 dinon tak ek jagah baithkar allaah kii ibaadat karte hai, jabaki mahilaayein ghar main rahakar hi ibaadat karti hai

 Unprecedented changes are coming in the way of work and the future of the workplace
 isamen aaj ausat rojgaar ke mukaable zyada lacheelaapan aa rahaa he
 The pwc study said that due to this change, in the next five years, employees will focus more on corporate value rather than salary
 peedblusi ke adhyayan ke mutabik do-tihaai karmchaaree yah maanate hai ki aajeevika kaa bhavi rasta karmchaaree swayan tay karenge na ki unki companiyaan
 According to the report, 63 percent of the surveyed people believe that the eight-hour work period will become obsolete, and 68 percent say that work can be done rather than working away from the traditional office
 peedblusi kii padmaja alaganandan ne kaha, 'yah saaf he ki kaam ke taur tareekon or kaarysthal ke bhavishya main baari badlaav aa rahaa he
 There is still a large portion of the workforce that prefers to operate in a traditional format while others are working as entrepreneurs and network-based models in which partners and partners are supported
 ' tippaniyan According to the survey, 86 percent people want to work independently because it is believed to have flexibility of time, control of the work environment, as well as opportunities for them to earn more and better balance between work and life
 Helps
 peedblusi ne is saal may main do online surveykshan kiye
 One was done with employees while the other with officers and executives who make decisions and directly change policies
 report ke mutabik survey main hissaa lene vaale 63 pratishat logon kaa maananaa he ki aath ghante kaam kii avadhi aprachlit ho jaaegi or 68 pratishat kaa kahana he ki paaramparik daftar ke jariye kaam karne ke bajaay kaam dur rahakar bhi kiya ja saktaa he
 pwc's Padmaja Alagandan said, "it is clear that there is a drastic change in the working practices and the future of the workplace
 abhi bhi kaarybal kaa bada hissaa he jo paaramparik swaroop main parichaalan karnaa pasand karata he jabaki anya udhyamiyon or network aadhaarit model ke taur par kaam kar rahe hai jisamen bhagidaaron or sahyogiyon kaa saath hota he
 Comments surveykshan ke mutabik 86 pratishat log swatantra hokar kaam karnaa chaahate hai kyonki iske bare main mana jaataa he ki isamen samay kaa lacheelaapan hota he, kaam ke maahaul par niyantran hota he iske saath hi unhen zyada kamaane ke maukey tathaa kaam or jivan ke bich behatar santulan main madad milti he
 pwc conducted two online surveys in May this year
